conversations on crisis management; to find ways to publicly intimate
that U.S. support for India during a crisis is in principle assured but
in practice not unbounded; and to encourage their Indian counterparts to
undertake realistic assessments of the value of military actions that
generate more political fervor than actual deterrence.]{.underline}
